msg:Let‚Äôs talk about what we are satisfied with first:
Selected Twin Rooms are upgraded to Selected Garden View Twin Rooms for free. The hotel is a garden-style house with few guest rooms, beautiful environment, strong sense of design and unique details, which is pleasing to the eye. The service staff are warm and friendly. Especially the bedding, I am very satisfied and it is very comfortable to sleep on! Can relax the whole body. The large rain shower in the bathroom is very comfortable. There is a coffee machine and the free coffee capsules are delicious. Automatic toilet seat heating is winter-friendly. I experienced it in the hotel restaurant in the morning, lunch and evening. The breakfast did not have an outstanding impression, and there was not much variety. The Chinese food for lunch was a la carte, and the dishes were exquisite and without fault. I ordered a Western set meal for two for dinner. I didn't expect that it was a double portion. It tasted pretty good. The steak was very thick and the presentation was exquisite. It was worth the price. I was quite impressed by this meal. The restaurant has an elegant environment, and the dining experience is good with fewer people at lunch and dinner.
The hotel room was on the small side, which was beyond my expectation. It seemed full with an extra bed, which was slightly inferior compared to other hotels of the same type. There is no makeup mirror. The quality of disposable items such as toothbrushes and combs provided by the hotel is not consistent with the hotel facilities. The toothbrushes are not comfortable to use and the combs have burrs that can pierce the scalp and pull the hair.
The number of steps taken in the Garden Expo every day is upwards of 10,000. At the end of the day, I am very tired and my whole body needs to relax. It's a pity that there is no massage spa anywhere. Maybe it‚Äôs because winter is approaching the New Year, the park is relatively desolate, and most restaurants are barely open. Eating is a problem.
In short, the hotel experience is not bad. It would be better if the extended services could be expanded.

posted:Posted May 15, 2022
msg:The main attractions are the 13 urban exhibition gardens. Adhering to the design concept of "reproducing the fine Jiangsu gardens with the old as the new", the historical gardens of seven cities in Nanjing, Wuxi, Changzhou, Suzhou, Huai'an, Yangzhou and Taizhou have been restored and combined with historical materials. Records and poetic situations recreated the garden architecture of six cities of Xuzhou, Nantong, Lianyungang, Yancheng, Zhenjiang and Suqian.
In addition to reproducing Jiangsu gardens, Jiangsu Garden Expo Park has also carried out ecological restoration in an all-round way, using industrial mines, small trains, etc., to create another "urban double repair" work. At the same time, the industrial relics in the jurisdiction will be reinforced, transformed and upgraded to form a green modern horticultural exhibition hall with complex functions.
